GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to determine if any candidate formula can be made equivalent to the GT:

$$f(x,t,v) = 0.156063 \sin(t) - 0.372948 \cdot v \cdot \exp(-|x|)$$

Key features of the GT:
1. A sinusoidal term in t: `sin(t)`
2. A term proportional to `v·exp(-|x|)` — note the absolute value of x

Let me analyze which candidates could potentially match.

**The critical challenge:** The GT contains `exp(-|x|)` multiplied by `v`. This is a non-analytic function in x (due to |x|). Most candidates use polynomial terms in x or smooth functions, which cannot replicate `exp(-|x|)` for all x.

Let me look for candidates that might have `exp(f(x))·v` type terms or could approximate `exp(-|x|)` exactly.

**Candidate 2:** Has `c3*exp(c4*x)*cos(c5*t)` and `c6*v` terms. The exp(c4*x) term isn't multiplied by v, and cos vs sin issue. Can't match.

**Candidate 17:** `c0*x² + c1*x + c2 + c3*v*x² + c4*cos(c5*t+c6) + c7*exp(c8*x)`. The exp term isn't multiplied by v. Can't match.

**Candidate 22:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2 + c3*x² + c4*v + c5*v²*x + c6*exp(c7*x)*cos(c8*t+c9)`. Has `exp(c7*x)*cos(c8*t+c9)` — this mixes x and t but not v. The v term is just `c4*v` (constant coefficient). Since we need `v*exp(-|x|)`, and `c4*v` only gives constant coefficient for v, this can't work for all x.

**Candidate 42:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2 + c3*v*x² + c4*exp(c5*x)*sin(c6*t+c7)`. Has `exp(c5*x)*sin(t)` which is good for the sin part (set c6=1, c7=0), but the v dependence is only through `c3*v*x²`, which can't match `v*exp(-|x|)`.

**Candidate 50:** `c6*exp(c7*x)*cos(c8*t+c9)` — again, exp·trig but no v coupling with exp.

**Candidate 45:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2+x)) + c3*x^c4*exp(c5*v) + c6*exp(c7*x)*sin(c8*t+c9)`. The term `c3*x^c4*exp(c5*v)` — this has exp(c5*v), not linear in v. Can't match v·exp(-|x|).

The fundamental problem is that `v·exp(-|x|)` requires:
1. A product of v with a function of |x|
2. The |x| makes it non-analytic at x=0

No candidate has a term like `v·exp(something with |x|)`. The candidates that have v multiplied by x-dependent terms use polynomials (v*x, v*x², v*x³) or nothing at all.

Some candidates have `v*Abs(v)` but that's different from what we need.

**Could any polynomial/exponential combination in x match exp(-|x|)?** No — exp(-|x|) is not analytic at x=0, so no finite combination of analytic functions can reproduce it. And polynomial terms certainly can't match it for all x.

None of the candidates contain a term of the form `v·f(|x|)` or `v·exp(-|x|)` that could reproduce the GT's behavior.

Even looking at candidates with general power terms like `x^c1` (candidates 8, 14, 26, 36, 41, 45, 48), these don't help because they're not multiplied by v in the right way, and `|x|` in the exponent can't be produced.

[NO MATCH]

No candidate formula can be made equivalent to the ground truth. The GT contains the term `v·exp(-|x|)`, which involves the absolute value function making it non-analytic at x=0. None of the candidates have a term that couples v with exp(-|x|) or any equivalent non-analytic function of x. The candidates either have v multiplied by polynomial functions of x (like v·x², v·x) or have exponential functions of x not coupled with v, making it impossible to reproduce the GT for all values of x, t, and v.

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (PO36)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: 0.156063*sin(t) - 0.372948*exp(-x)*v**

where x > 0 (so |x| = x), t ≥ 0.

The GT has two terms:
1. A sinusoidal term in t: `F0*sin(t)`
2. A term `−beta*exp(−x)*v` — this is v multiplied by an exponential decay in x.

Key structural requirements:
- The v-dependence is **linear** (just v times a function of x)
- The x-dependence in the v-term is `exp(-x)`, which is NOT a polynomial, rational function, or power law
- The t-dependence is `sin(t)` (or equivalently `cos(t + phase)`)

Let me analyze each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x/(c1+x) + c2*v*|v| + c3*x + c4*cos(c5*t+c6) + c7*v + c8*v*x² + c9*v*x`
The v-dependent terms are: c2*v*|v|, c7*v, c8*v*x², c9*v*x. The GT needs v*exp(-x). We'd need c2=0 (to kill |v| term), then we have v*(c7 + c8*x² + c9*x), a polynomial in x times v. But exp(-x) is not a polynomial. Also c0*x/(c1+x) + c3*x are x-only terms that GT doesn't have (GT has no x-only terms besides through v). Setting c0=c3=0 removes those, but v*(polynomial in x) ≠ v*exp(-x).
**Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 2:** `c0 + c1*x + c2*v³ + c3*exp(c4*x)*cos(c5*t) + c6*v + c7*cos(c8*t+c9)`
This has exp(c4*x)*cos(c5*t) which mixes x and t. The GT has no such mixed term. Setting c3=0 kills it, but then we only have c6*v for v-dependence (no exp(-x) factor). Can't match.
Wait - could c3*exp(c4*x)*cos(c5*t) somehow help? It doesn't involve v at all. The GT's v*exp(-x) term requires v. Setting c2=0 (kill v³), we have c6*v which is just linear in v with no x-dependence. Can't produce v*exp(-x).
**Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 3:** `c0 + c1*x + c2*v³ + c3*cos(c4*t+c5) + c6*v + c7*v*x`
